      <script type="text/javascript">
(function($){
    function getNextFeatureId() {
        var current = parseInt($('#home-fresh-pix .controls .current').index()) + 1;
        if (current < 1 || current >= totalFeatures) {
            current = 0;
        }
		current++;
        return 'freshPix' + current;
    }

    function loadFeature(fromControl, featureId) {
		if (fromControl !== true) {
			featureId = getNextFeatureId();
		} else {
		    if ($('#home-fresh-pix .controls .current').attr('id') == featureId) {
		        return;
		    }
		}
        $('#home-fresh-pix .images .current,#home-fresh-pix .titles .current').hide().removeClass('current');
        $('#home-fresh-pix .images .' + featureId + ',#home-fresh-pix .titles .' + featureId).fadeIn(200).addClass('current');
        $('#home-fresh-pix .controls .current').removeClass('current');
        $('#home-fresh-pix .controls #' + featureId).addClass('current');
    }

    $('#home-fresh-pix .controls li').click(function() {
        loadFeature(true, $(this).attr('id'));
    });

    $('#home-fresh-pix .images').hover(function() {
        //clearInterval(autorun);
    }, function() {
        //autorun = setInterval(loadFeature, speed);
    });

    /*
    $(window).focus(function() {
        if (!autorun)
            autorun = setInterval(loadFeature, speed);
    });

    $(window).blur(function() {
        clearInterval(autorun);
        autorun = 0;
    });
    */

    //var speed = 5000;
    //var autorun = setInterval(loadFeature, speed);
    var totalFeatures = $('#home-fresh-pix .controls li').length;

})( jQuery );
</script>

         <div class="title">
          <h2><a href="http://www.extratv.com/2014/03/11/true-detective-2-preview-at-least-how-jimmy-kimmel-and-seth-rogen-see-it/">‘True Detective 2’ Preview… At Least How Jimmy Kimmel and Seth Rogen See It</a></h2>
         </div> 
         <div class="publish-info"> 
          <span class="publish-date">March 11, 2014</span> 
          <span class="category"><a href="http://www.extratv.com/category/television/">Television</a></span> 
         </div> 
         <div class="sharing sharing-top clearfix"> 
          <span class="st_fblike_hcount" displaytext="Facebook" st_url="http://www.extratv.com/2014/03/11/true-detective-2-preview-at-least-how-jimmy-kimmel-and-seth-rogen-see-it/" st_title="‘True Detective 2’ Preview… At Least How Jimmy Kimmel and Seth Rogen See It"></span> 
          <span class="st_twitter_hcount" displaytext="Tweet" st_via="extratv" st_url="http://www.extratv.com/2014/03/11/true-detective-2-preview-at-least-how-jimmy-kimmel-and-seth-rogen-see-it/" st_title="‘True Detective 2’ Preview… At Least How Jimmy Kimmel and Seth Rogen See It"></span> 
          <span class="st_plusone_hcount" displaytext="Google +" st_url="http://www.extratv.com/2014/03/11/true-detective-2-preview-at-least-how-jimmy-kimmel-and-seth-rogen-see-it/" st_title="‘True Detective 2’ Preview… At Least How Jimmy Kimmel and Seth Rogen See It"></span> 
         </div> 
         <div class="contents clearfix">
           Late-night talk show host Jimmy Kimmel and pal Seth Rogen spoof “True Detective,” as only they can.
          <br />
          <br />As fans of the show know, neither Matthew McConaughey nor Woody Harrelson will be back for the HBO show’s second season, which leaves the door open for Rogen and Kimmel to pick up where the first season left off.
          <br />
          <br />This, of course, means the two must make out at some point.
          <br />
          <br />Watch Kimmel’s trailer for &quot;True Detective 2.&quot;
          <br />
          <br />
          <iframe width="560" height="315" style="display: block; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;" src="//www.youtube.com/embed/d35uzpO3Al4" frameborder="0" allowfullscreen=""></iframe>
          <br />&quot;Extra&quot; caught up with Kimmel at SXSW, where the late-night host has been doing his show. 
          <p>Jimmy opened up about becoming a father again with wife Molly. “My youngest son is 20 years old, I’m going to have to learn things and things have changed… It’s interesting like every ten years there seems to be a new approach, I’m going to have to learn things or just hope my wife does.”</p> 
          <p>Kimmel said Molly is feeling better after battling morning sickness. The couple doesn’t plan on finding out the gender of the baby, saying, “We don’t know, we’re not finding out.”</p> 
          <p>Jimmy also joked about his comedic feud with Matt Damon, saying, “Damon is not getting anywhere near that kid, I don’t care if he does own a zoo.”<br /><br />When the conversation turned to Jimmy Fallon and the &quot;Tonight Show,&quot; Kimmel said he keeps an eye on what the other late-night shows are doing. “Of course we watch, believe me, we watch each other like hawks.”&nbsp;&nbsp;</p> 
          <div class="primary-video-embed" id="primary-video-embed-0_gfpww9x0"> 
           <object id="kaltura_player_0_gfpww9x0" name="kaltura_player_0_gfpww9x0" type="application/x-shockwave-flash" allowfullscreen="true" allownetworking="all" allowscriptaccess="always" flashvars="" wmode="transparent" width="480" height="316" bgcolor="#000000" xmlns:dc="http://purl.org/dc/terms/" xmlns:media="http://search.yahoo.com/searchmonkey/media/" rel="media:video" resource="http://www.kaltura.com/index.php/kwidget/cache_st/1312495109/wid/_594231/uiconf_id/5394821/entry_id/0_gfpww9x0" data="http://www.kaltura.com/index.php/kwidget/cache_st/1312495109/wid/_594231/uiconf_id/5394821/entry_id/0_gfpww9x0"> <param name="allowFullScreen" value="true"></param> <param name="allowNetworking" value="all"></param> <param name="allowScriptAccess" value="always"></param> <param name="wmode" value="transparent"></param> <param name="bgcolor" value="#000000"></param> <param name="flashVars" value=""></param> <param name="movie" value="http://www.kaltura.com/index.php/kwidget/cache_st/1312495109/wid/_594231/uiconf_id/5394821/entry_id/0_gfpww9x0"></param> <a rel="media:thumbnail" href="http://cdnbakmi.kaltura.com/p/594231/sp/59423100/thumbnail/entry_id/0_gfpww9x0/width/120/height/90/bgcolor/000000/type/2"></a> <span property="media:width" content="480"></span> <span property="media:height" content="316"></span> <span property="media:type" content="application/x-shockwave-flash"></span> </object> 
           <div id="adCompanionBanner0_gfpww9x0" class="adCompanionBanner"></div> 
          </div> 
          <p>Jimmy will be back with more jokes from Austin Tuesday night on ABC.</p> 
         </div> 
         <div class="readmore">
          <a href="http://www.extratv.com/2014/03/11/true-detective-2-preview-at-least-how-jimmy-kimmel-and-seth-rogen-see-it/">Read More &raquo;</a>

         </div> 
         <div class="sharing sharing-top clearfix"> 
          <span class="st_fblike_hcount" displaytext="Facebook" st_url="http://www.extratv.com/2014/03/11/must-see-video-president-obama-sits-between-two-ferns-with-zach-galifianakis/" st_title="Must-See Video! President Obama Sits ‘Between Two Ferns’ with Zach Galifianakis"></span> 
          <span class="st_twitter_hcount" displaytext="Tweet" st_via="extratv" st_url="http://www.extratv.com/2014/03/11/must-see-video-president-obama-sits-between-two-ferns-with-zach-galifianakis/" st_title="Must-See Video! President Obama Sits ‘Between Two Ferns’ with Zach Galifianakis"></span> 
          <span class="st_plusone_hcount" displaytext="Google +" st_url="http://www.extratv.com/2014/03/11/must-see-video-president-obama-sits-between-two-ferns-with-zach-galifianakis/" st_title="Must-See Video! President Obama Sits ‘Between Two Ferns’ with Zach Galifianakis"></span> 
         </div> 
         <div class="contents clearfix">
           In a bid to encourage young people to sign up for health insurance, President Barack Obama continued to show his cool side by appearing on the hilarious FunnyorDie.com show “Between Two Ferns,” with host Zach Galifianakis.
          <br />
          <br />As per the show’s setup, Obama was ready for Galifianakis’ awkwardness… and barbs. When Galifianakis asked him, “What’s it like to be the last black president,” Obama quipped, “Seriously? What’s it like for this to be that last time you ever talk to a president?”
          <br />
          <br />You can’t miss this one… watch!
          <br />
          <br /> 
          <iframe width="640" height="400" style="display: block; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;" src="http://www.funnyordie.com/embed/18e820ec3f" frameborder="0" allowfullscreen="" webkitallowfullscreen="" mozallowfullscreen=""></iframe> 
         </div> 
         <div class="readmore">
          <a href="http://www.extratv.com/2014/03/11/must-see-video-president-obama-sits-between-two-ferns-with-zach-galifianakis/">Read More &raquo;</a>

         <div class="title">
          <h2><a href="http://www.extratv.com/2014/03/11/justin-bieber-and-selena-gomez-steam-up-the-dance-floor-in-this-sexy-routine/">Justin Bieber and Selena Gomez Steam Up the Dance Floor in This Sexy Routine! </a></h2>
         </div> 
         <div class="publish-info"> 
          <span class="publish-date">March 11, 2014</span> 
          <span class="category"><a href="http://www.extratv.com/category/top-stories/">Top Stories</a></span> 
         </div> 
         <div class="sharing sharing-top clearfix"> 
          <span class="st_fblike_hcount" displaytext="Facebook" st_url="http://www.extratv.com/2014/03/11/justin-bieber-and-selena-gomez-steam-up-the-dance-floor-in-this-sexy-routine/" st_title="Justin Bieber and Selena Gomez Steam Up the Dance Floor in This Sexy Routine! "></span> 
          <span class="st_twitter_hcount" displaytext="Tweet" st_via="extratv" st_url="http://www.extratv.com/2014/03/11/justin-bieber-and-selena-gomez-steam-up-the-dance-floor-in-this-sexy-routine/" st_title="Justin Bieber and Selena Gomez Steam Up the Dance Floor in This Sexy Routine! "></span> 
          <span class="st_plusone_hcount" displaytext="Google +" st_url="http://www.extratv.com/2014/03/11/justin-bieber-and-selena-gomez-steam-up-the-dance-floor-in-this-sexy-routine/" st_title="Justin Bieber and Selena Gomez Steam Up the Dance Floor in This Sexy Routine! "></span> 
         </div> 
         <div class="contents clearfix"> 
          <p class="p1">Looks like pop stars Justin Bieber, 20, and Selena Gomez, 21, are rekindling their romance, and in the sexiest way possible!</p> 
          <div class="primary-image primary-image-portrait"> 
           <div class="image"> 
            <a href="http://www.extratv.com/2014/03/11/justin-bieber-and-selena-gomez-steam-up-the-dance-floor-in-this-sexy-routine/"><img src="http://cdn-media.extratv.com/2014/03/11/justin-bieber-450x600.jpg" width="450" alt="Justin Bieber and Selena Gomez Steam Up the Dance Floor in This Sexy Routine! " border="0" /></a> 
           </div> 
          </div> Watch the dynamic duo take their moves to the dance floor in this choreographed routine to Ordinary People by John Legend. 
         </div> 
         <div class="readmore">
          <a href="http://www.extratv.com/2014/03/11/justin-bieber-and-selena-gomez-steam-up-the-dance-floor-in-this-sexy-routine/">Read More &raquo;</a>

            <div id="action-panel-details" class="action-panel-content "> 
             <div id="watch-description" class="yt-uix-expander yt-uix-expander-collapsed yt-uix-button-panel"> 
              <div id="watch-description-content"> 
               <div id="watch-description-clip"> 
                <p id="watch-uploader-info"> <strong>Published on <span id="eow-date" class="watch-video-date">May 10, 2013</span> </strong> </p> 
                <div id="watch-description-text"> 
                 <p id="eow-description">Looking at any given image or video sequence, Amit Roy-Chowdhury is looking to understand the content. Similar to the brain's processing and interpreting of images, his research seeks to develop automated algorithms that not only capture and store images, but understand the content of those images. Prof. Roy-Chowdhury's research has been supported by various agencies including the National Science Foundation, Office of Naval Research, Army Research Office, DARPA, National Endowment for the Humanities, and private industries like CISCO and Lockheed-Martin. His recent book on Camera Networks provides an overview of current research in the field.</p> 
                </div> 
                <div id="watch-description-extras">

                   </div> </li> 
                  <li> <h4 class="title">License</h4> 
                   <div class="content"> 
                    <p id="eow-reuse"> Standard YouTube License </p> 
                   </div> </li> 
                 </ul>

        $(function () {
            $("#txtGoogleSearch").each(function () {
                ToggleHint($(this)); // add class on page load to elements with "hintable" class
            });

            $("#txtGoogleSearch").focus(function () {
                $(this).removeClass("GoogleWatermark"); // handle all focus hints
            });

            $("#txtGoogleSearch").blur(function () {
                ToggleHint(this); // handle all blur hints
            });
        });

        function ToggleHint(obj) {
            if ($(obj).val() == '') { $(obj).addClass("GoogleWatermark"); };
        }

     <img src="/Images/reports.png" alt="" class="page-lead" /> 
     <div class="span-11"> 
      <h3>Preparers: Request Reports</h3> 
      <p> Depending on your proposal, you may need to request mandatory reports. The purpose of ordering reports is to show you which courses and majors would be impacted by your course proposal. Responding appropriately to reports ensures that all impacted courses and programs stay current. </p> 
     </div> 
     <div class="span-11"> 
      <div class="accordion" style="margin-right: 5px;"> 
       <h4><img src="/Images/square-bullet.png" alt="" />Do I need to request reports?</h4> 
       <div class="addBullet"> 
        <p>You must request reports if you are:</p> 
        <ul> 
         <li>Deleting a course</li> 
         <li>Renumbering a course</li> 
         <li>Changing a course title</li> 
         <li>Changing the units</li> 
         <li>Changing a cross-listing</li> 
         <li>Changing a credit statement</li> 
         <li>Submitting a course proposal with an enrollment priority statement or restriction</li> 
        </ul> 
       </div> 
       <h4><img src="/Images/square-bullet.png" alt="" />Why?</h4> 
       <p>It may seem like several extra steps to run the required reports, but they are critical to ensuring that ALL courses and programs that are impacted by your course proposal stay current.</p> 
       <h4><img src="/Images/square-bullet.png" alt="" />When?</h4> 
       <p>You must request reports before you submit your course proposal in CRAMS and at least five working days before a <a href="http://senate.ucr.edu/committee/8/Submission Deadlines for 2014-15.pdf" class="noUnderline" target="_blank">submission deadline</a>. If you are late, you must <a href="http://senate.ucr.edu/committee/8/request_for_extension_of_course_proposal_submission_deadline_form.html" class="noUnderline" target="_blank">request an extension</a>. </p> 
       <h4><img src="/Images/square-bullet.png" alt="" />How?</h4> 
       <div> 
        <p> Complete this online form. Enter the subject code and course number(s). You may enter as many course numbers as the field can handle, just make sure to separate them with commas. Check all the boxes that apply to your proposal. When you have entered all subject codes, proposed actions and required fields, hit &quot;submit.&quot; </p> 
        <p> Then, the Academic Senate and/or Academic Scheduling will run the appropriate report(s) for you. You will receive an email outlining the results. After that, you should take the appropriate steps based on your proposal’s impact (contacting departments with cross-listed courses etc.). </p> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <br /> 
     </div> 
     <div class="span-7 last">

     <div class="span-11 last"> 
      <h3>After You Receive Your Reports: </h3> 
      <ol class="marginBtmMenu10Li"> 
       <li>Complete the appropriate fields in CRAMS on the Other Courses/Programs tab.</li> 
       <li>Prepare course proposals for your department’s affected courses and submit them concurrently. </li> 
       <li>Submit program changes for your department's affected majors, minors, and programs. </li> 
       <li>Contact other departments immediately if their courses, majors, minors, or programs are affected. <a href="../../Content/pdfs/Find_a_Preparer.pdf" target="_blank" class="noUnderline">Find department preparers.</a></li> 
       <li>Document course and program changes internally to facilitate updating general catalog proofs.</li> 
       <li><a class="noUnderline" href="/crams/support-services/default.aspx">Contact us</a> if you have questions. </li> 
      </ol> 
     </div>

   <div id="content"> 
    <h2>Organizational Structure</h2> 
    <!-- Start Sidebar --> 
    <div id="sidebar"> 
     <div class="nav"> 
      <h3 class="accessibility">Main Navigation</h3> 
      <ul> 
       <li><a href="/" title="Home">Home<br /><span></span></a></li>
       <li><a href="/accre_process.html" title="Accreditation Process">Accreditation Process<br /><span></span></a></li>
       <li class="currentpage"><h3><dfn>Current page is: </dfn>Organizational Structure</h3></li>
       <li><a href="/proposal_accre.html" title="Proposal for Accreditation">Proposal for Accreditation<br /><span></span></a></li>
       <li><a href="/prep_review_report.html" title="Preparatory Review Report">Preparatory Review Report<br /><span></span></a></li>
       <li><a href="/eer.html" title="Educational Effectiveness Report">Educational Effectiveness Report</a></li>
       <li><a href="/wascvisit.html" title="WASC Team Visit Reports">WASC Team Visit Reports<br /><span></span></a></li>
       <li><a href="/timeline_reaccre.html" title="Timeline for UCR Reaccreditation">Timeline for UCR Reaccreditation<br /><span></span></a></li>
       <li><a href="/learningoutcomes.html" title="Learning Outcomes Assessment">Learning Outcomes Assessment<br /><span></span></a></li>

    <hr /> 
    <!-- End Sidebar --> 
    <!-- Start Content Area --> 
    <div id="main"> 
     <!-- com.omniupdate.editor csspath="/z-omniupdate/css/content.css" cssmenu="" width="790" --> 
     <div id="omnicontent">
      <br />The Chancellor is ultimately responsible for UCR's reaccreditation process; in 2004, then Chancellor France C&oacute;rdova delegated that responsibility to then Executive Vice Chancellor/Provost Ellen Wartella, who appointed a Steering Committee and Subcommittees to guide the process. Currently, Chancellor Timothy P. White and Executive Vice Chancellor/Provost Dallas Rabenstein kept the same steering committee and subcommittee structure.&nbsp; The UCR Accreditation Liaison Officer (ALO) is the official representative of the campus to WASC and the person through whom communication between WASC and UCR takes place. Steven Brint, Vice Provost for Undergraduate Education, is UCR's ALO and can be reached via telephone at 951-827-7750. 
      <h5><strong>Appointment of UCR WASC Steering Committee:</strong></h5> 
      <p>In November 2004 Executive Vice Chancellor/Provost Ellen Wartella appointed a WASC Steering Committee, currently co-chaired by Professor&nbsp;Eugene Nothnagel&nbsp;and Vice Provost Yolanda Moses, to plan and oversee the upcoming cycle of WASC reaccreditation.</p> 
      <p><span style="text-decoration: underline;"><strong>WASC Steering Committee Membership (2009-10)</strong></span></p> 
      <ul> 
       <li>Eugene Nothnagel, Faculty Co-Chair, Professor of Plant Physiology</li> 
       <li>Yolanda Moses, Administrative Co-Chair, Vice Provost for Conflict Resolution and<br />Associate Vice Chancellor for Excellence and Diversity</li> 
       <li>Gary Coyne, Graduate Student Association (GSA) President</li> 
       <li>Stephen Cullenberg, Dean, College of Humanities, Arts and Social Sciences</li> 
       <li>Bob Daly, Assistant Vice Chancellor for Academic Planning and Budget</li> 
       <li>Sharon Duffy, Faculty Representative, Professor of Education</li> 
       <li>David Fairris, Vice Provost for Undergraduate Education</li> 
       <li>John Gary, Faculty Representative, Professor of Physics and Astronomy</li> 
       <li>Robert Gill, Special Consultant</li> 
       <li>Tom Lutz, Faculty Representative, Professor of Creative Writing</li> 
       <li>Jessica Maldonado, ASUCR President</li> 
       <li>Thomas Payne, Faculty Co-Chair of Educational Effectiveness Subcommittee, Associate Professor of Computer Science</li> 
       <li>Veronica Ruiz, Staff Assembly President, AVC -- Enrollment Department</li> 
       <li>James Sandoval, Vice Chancellor for Student Affairs</li> 
      </ul> 
      <p>Faculty representatives were suggested by the Academic Senate Committee on Committees, undergraduate and graduate student representatives were suggested by the ASUCR and GSA, and the staff representative was suggested by the Staff Assembly.</p> 
      <h5><strong>Subcommittees of UCR WASC Steering Committee:</strong></h5> 
      <p>Two subcommittees were established in February 2005, one on Institutional Capacity and one on Educational Effectiveness.</p> 
      <p><span style="text-decoration: underline;"><strong>WASC Institutional Capacity Subcommittee</strong></span></p> 
      <p>The Institutional Capacity Subcommittee completed its tasks with the preparation of the Preparatory Review Report and the coordination of the follow up WASC visit, so it has been disbanded.</p> 
      <h5>Institutional Capacity Subcommittee Purpose:</h5> 
      <ul> 
       <li>Develop Evidence to Demonstrate Compliance with the Four WASC Standards 
        <ul> 
         <li>Defining Institutional Purposes and Ensuring Educational Objectives</li> 
         <li>Achieving Educational Objectives through Core Functions</li> 
         <li>Developing and Applying Resources and Organizational Structures to Ensure Sustainability</li> 
         <li>Creating an Organization Committed to Learning and Improvement</li> 
        </ul> </li> 
       <li>Assure that UCR has effective data gathering and analysis systems</li> 
       <li>Prepare the <a href="/prep_review_report.html">Preparatory Review Report</a> 
        <ul> 
         <li>Reflective and Concluding Essays corresponding to the WASC Standards</li> 
         <li>Institutional Portfolio of descriptive data, policies, exhibits, and data displays</li> 
         <li>Appendix with Institutional Response to previous team recommendations</li> 
         <li>Maximum of 35 pages, exclusive of exhibits and appendices</li> 
         <li>Posted for General Campus Comment on November 14, 2007</li> 
         <li>General Campus Comments were due by December 5, 2007</li> 
         <li>Submitted to WASC on December 20, 2007</li> 
         <li>Was followed by a WASC site visit March 12-14, 2008</li> 
        </ul> </li> 
      </ul> 
      <h5>WASC Educational Effectiveness Subcommittee</h5> 
      <p>The Educational Effectiveness Subcommittee completed its tasks with the preparation of the Educational Effectiveness Report and the coordination of the follow up WASC visit, so it has been disbanded.</p> 
      <h5>Educational Effectiveness Subcommittee Purpose:</h5> 
      <ul> 
       <li>In depth study of three special themes:<br /> 
        <ul> 
         <li>Learning within a Campus Culture of Diversity</li> 
         <li>Growing and Improving Graduate and Professional Programs</li> 
         <li>Improving Undergraduate Student Engagement, Experience, and Learning Outcomes</li> 
        </ul> </li> 
       <li>Thorough assessment of UCR compliance with four WASC Standards<br /> 
        <ul> 
         <li>Defining Institutional Purposes and Ensuring Educational Objectives</li> 
         <li>Achieving Educational Objectives through Core Functions</li> 
         <li>Developing and Applying Resources and Organizational Structures to Ensure Sustainability</li> 
         <li>Creating an Organization Committed to Learning and Improvement</li> 
        </ul> </li> 
       <li>Preparing the Educational Effectiveness Report<br /> 
        <ul> 
         <li>Description of the Educational Effectiveness Approach</li> 
         <li>Deep engagement and analysis of Educational Effectiveness, including analytical essays regarding the special themes</li> 
         <li>Supportive evidence for the analysis of Educational Effectiveness, building on the institutional portfolio prepared for the Preparatory Review</li> 
         <li>An integrative component</li> 
         <li>Maximum of 50 pages, exclusive of exhibits</li> 
         <li>Was submitted July 7, 2009</li> 
         <li>Was followed by WASC site visit October 27-29, 2009</li> 
        </ul> </li> 
      </ul> 
      <p align="right"><a onclick="window.scrollTo(0,0); return false" href="#">Back to Top</a></p>
